52b4(ja7): bsdu bgrigs byed pa'o ga rkabs kyi ched yug de tsam byung med pas/ 'did phyogs la nyams myeng dang lag len segs la mig zhes len gzhi dken pas gam cha gsad du yin pa dang / sghes su de zhus bgrigs pa che / 
52b5(ja7): yang mkhyen dbyed dab 'byams pa min thad/ 'di' thad mthun rkyen zung la 'gal rkyen mang ba'i gseb ru dal brling 'grig s dang la byung na/ phyegs gang so'i thad yug dang gnas sangs tsha las brgal ba'i legs cha / 
52b6(ja7): zhig then thabs med pas/ de lugs kyis rjes su gzigs mthan rnam pas 'di la dg rkyen thad ye bsrang yong nges gnang de che zhing / 'di yi byas pa 'dis kyang sad du g.yung dung ben gyi lung gi bstan pa don po me gsal
